When checking in, because the weather suddenly warmed up, the gentleman at the front desk arranged a room on a high floor with a lake view and away from the sun. The room attendants were enthusiastic and made the turndown at night. When making the turndown, they would add paper towels + bottled drinking water, etc. according to the situation of the room; in the evening, the room would be given desserts, Tremella and peach gum soup, and the desserts were served in small bowls with covers, which was quite high-quality. The swimming pool has a suitable temperature, and the water is clean and refreshing without the smell of chlorine. In fact, the front desk called at 13:00 to urge check-out, which affected the overall arrangement. There is room for improvement in the details of the front desk service.
